QUESTIONS: 1. Are students living in the village more successful than
those living in the city center?

Answer 1

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Number of successful students (1) living in Village (0)}

\CommentTok{\#df$IKAMET}
\CommentTok{\#df$Başarılı.Mı}
\NormalTok{koyDf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(df, IKAMET }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{basariliDf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(df, Başarılı.Mı }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{koyIntersectDf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{intersect}\NormalTok{(koyDf, basariliDf)}
\CommentTok{\# Intersection df}

\CommentTok{\#data.frame(koyIntersectDf$IKAMET, koyIntersectDf$Başarılı.Mı)}

\NormalTok{koyBasariliSayisi }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(koyIntersectDf)}

\CommentTok{\# Number of successful students (1) living in the center (1)}
\NormalTok{merkezDf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(df, IKAMET }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{merkezIntersectDf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{intersect}\NormalTok{(merkezDf, basariliDf)}
\CommentTok{\# Intersection df}

\CommentTok{\#data.frame(merkezIntersectDf$IKAMET, merkezIntersectDf$Başarılı.Mı)}

\NormalTok{merkezBasariliSayisi }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(merkezIntersectDf)}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (koyBasariliSayisi }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}}\NormalTok{ merkezBasariliSayisi) \{}
  \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Students living in the village are more successful."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Students living in the city center are more successful."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] "Students living in the city center are more successful."
\end{verbatim}
